      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n9572-2" target="تحوّل" n="2" type="1" subtype="SO" lang="ar" select="n9576"/></foreign>; (K:) which [here] signifies [as above; or] <hi rend="ital">it became altered, transmuted,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">changed,</hi> whether <hi rend="ital">essentially</hi> or <hi rend="ital">substantially,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">in respect of predicament</hi> [or <hi rend="ital">state</hi> or <hi rend="ital">condition</hi>], or <hi rend="ital">by saying;</hi> (Er-Rághib, TA;) and

(IAar, TA.)          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  [Hence, also,] <foreign lang="ar">حال</foreign>, inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">مَحَالٌ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">حِيلَةٌ</foreign>, <hi rend="ital">i. q.</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">احتال</foreign>, q. v. (Ham p. 652.)          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  And <foreign lang="ar">حال</foreign> and
